        function centerImage() {
          var $ = ___saveJQFromPrototype;
          // center the masthead image vertically:

         <script type="text/javascript">
          var spinner = $('&lt;img style="position:relative;top:3px;left:5px;" class="admin-ajax-spinner" src="/static/img/spinner.gif" /&gt;');
    var successCallback = function($el, data) {
      var parsedData = JSON.parse(data);

      if (parsedData['messages']) {
        if (parsedData['messages'].length &gt; 0) {
          alert(parsedData['messages'][0]);
          $el.parents('div.entryList').hide();
        }
        else {
          alert('An unknown error occurred.');
        }
      }
      else {
        alert('An unknown error occurred.');
      }

      $('.admin-ajax-spinner').remove();

    };

    $('.delete-topic').click(function(e) {

      $(this).parents('div.topics-admin-options').append(spinner);

      var dataPayload = {
        posted: new Date().getTime(),
        topicId: $(this).data('id'),
        areyousure: 'yes'
      },
      $this = $(this),
      callback = function(data) {
        return successCallback($this, data);
      };

      $.post('/edit/delete', dataPayload, callback);

    });

    $('.limbo-topic').click(function(e) {

      $(this).parents('div.topics-admin-options').append(spinner);

      var dataPayload = {
        posted: new Date().getTime(),
        objectIds: $(this).data('id'),
        action: 'LIMBO',
        type: 'T'
      },
      $this = $(this),
      callback = function(data) {
        return successCallback($this, data);
      };

      $.post('/admin/quarantine', dataPayload, callback);

    });
         </script>

      <p id="GRP-authorByline">
       <img class="group_sidebar_img_8" src="http://cdn.instructables.com/F9V/A781/H5JVOPKU/F9VA781H5JVOPKU.TINY.jpg"/>
       Moderated group created by
       <a class="group_sidebar_a_9" href="/member/ReadySet/" id="GRP-authorLink" title="view ReadySet's profile">
        ReadySet
       </a>
       on Aug 3, 2012
      </p>
      <br/>
      <div id="GRP-bodyText">
       <style type="text/css">
        #group-body {
    background-color:#a2becf;
}
       </style>
       Energy is everything and pretty much everywhere. But this doesnt mean that everyone has access to electricity. Thats what we do. We create renewable energy products for the 1.5 billion who live off-the-grid in developing countries. This is why were inviting you to create projects that harness energy from renewable and natural resources such as the sun, wind, and water.
       <br/>
       <br/>
       To help you start creating, weve published the technical specifications for our Fenix ReadySet so you can get an idea of the sources of power generation and applications we develop on our end. In short, the ReadySet's intelligent battery allows you to charge from virtually any source such as solar panels, bicycle generators, and micro-wind turbines, to power all kinds of devices from its two open standard 12-volt Car Lighter Adapter ports and two 5-volt USB ports.
       <br/>
       <br/>
      </div>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   ___saveJQFromPrototype(document).ready(function() {
        var $ = ___saveJQFromPrototype;


        // assign IDs to each tab button and corresponding IDs to each tab pane
        $(".tabgroup-button").each( function(index) {
            $(this).attr('id','tab-button-'+index)
        });
        $(".tab-pane").each (function(index) {
            $(this).attr('id','tab-pane-'+index)
        });

        // click handler for tab buttons:
        $(".tabgroup-button").click(function(){
            var indexToShow = $(this).attr('id').substr(11);
            switchPanes($("#tab-pane-"+indexToShow));
            $(".tabgroup-button").not($(this)).removeClass('tabgroup-button-selected');
            $(this).addClass('tabgroup-button-selected');
        });

        // hide and show corresponding tabs
        function switchPanes(jqueryObj) {
            // hides all non-selected panes, then shows the requested one
            $(".tab-pane").not(jqueryObj).hide();
            jqueryObj.show();
        };

        $('.enterInstructable').click(function(){
            var groupCategory = $(this).parents('.image-display-wrapper-styleC').find('select').val();
            var alertText = "Your Instructable has been added to the group";
            if (true) {alertText += ", but the group moderator needs to give it the ok before it will show up.";}
            var id = $(this).parents('.image-display-wrapper-styleC').attr('id');
            var that=$(this);
            $('#addId').val(id); $('#removeId').val("");
            $('#groupCategory').val(groupCategory);
            $.ajax({
              type: 'POST',
              url: "/group/addinstructable",
              data: $('#EnterForm').serialize(),
              success: function() {alert(alertText);that.css('color','#999999');that.unbind(); }
            });
        });

        $('.removeInstructable').click(function(){
            var alertText = "Your Instructable will be removed from the group";
            var id = $(this).parents('.image-display-wrapper-styleC').attr('id');
            var that=$(this);
            $('#addId').val(""); $('#removeId').val(id);

            $.ajax({
              type: 'POST',
              url: "/group/addinstructable",
              data: $('#EnterForm').serialize(),
              success: function() {alert(alertText);that.css('color','#999999');that.unbind(); }
            });
        }); 
        
        


    });
  </script>
